<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Supranational_bodies">Supranational bodies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Supranational bodies">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3072" data-file-width="4608" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/220px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/330px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg/440px-Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tacloban_Typhoon_Haiyan_2013-11-14.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Debris littering the streets of Tacloban City on November 14, nearly a week after the storm struck.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1944" data-file-width="2592" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/220px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/330px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG/440px-Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Basey_after_Yolanda2.JPG" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Devastation in the town of <a href="/wiki/Basey,_Samar" title="Basey, Samar">Basey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samar" title="Samar">Samar</a>, where more than 300 individuals perished due to storm surge.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The United Nations said it was going to increase critical relief operations as a result of the devastation caused by the typhoon. Its Manila office issued a statement that read, "Access remains a key challenge as some areas are still cut off from relief operations. Unknown numbers of survivors do not have basic necessities such as food, water and medicines and remain inaccessible for relief operations, as roads, airports and bridges were destroyed or covered in wreckage."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216"><a href="#cite_note-216">[212]</a></sup> The United Nations also began relief operations by this time; however, the severe damage to infrastructure hampered efforts to distribute supplies.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CBSNov10_106-1"><a href="#cite_note-CBSNov10-106">[102]</a></sup> The UN activated the Cluster System, in which groups of humanitarian organizations (UN and non-UN) work to restore health, shelter, nutrition and economic activity.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217"><a href="#cite_note-217">[213]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a>, which leads the Health Cluster, the largest one, has developed guidance on donations of medicine and healthcare equipment, so that the Philippines receives supplies appropriate for this emergency. According to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WHO" title="WHO">WHO</a>, many people suffered cuts, wounds, and broken bones during the disaster and others were injured in flooding that followed the typhoon.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218"><a href="#cite_note-218">[214]</a></sup> Interpol announced that they would send in Interpol officers from Lyon to help local law enforcement identify any of the corpses that are unidentified.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219"><a href="#cite_note-219">[215]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> has spearheaded initiatives among help workers, especially from the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Health_(Philippines)" title="Department of Health (Philippines)">Department of Health (Philippines)</a>, in extending Psychological First Aid to people in typhoon-affected areas. WHO Representative in the country Dr <a href="/wiki/Julie_Hall" title="Julie Hall">Julie Hall</a> foresees long-lasting effects from the typhoon. She calls for increased preparedness to give support to families and communities for the long-term, citing the need for more trained field workers.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220"><a href="#cite_note-220">[216]</a></sup></p>
<h4><span id="Celebrities,_companies,_and_NGOs"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Celebrities.2C_companies.2C_and_NGOs">Celebrities, companies, and NGOs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Celebrities, companies, and NGOs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>American band <a href="/wiki/Journey_(band)" title="Journey (band)">Journey</a> donated $350,000 to help relief efforts in the Philippines, and its lead singer had a message for his homeland: "Don't Stop Believin'". <a href="/wiki/Arnel_Pineda" title="Arnel Pineda">Arnel Pineda</a> (the band's Filipino vocalist) and the rest of the band announced the donation on November 15, 2013. It will go to the United Nations World Food Programme, which is providing Filipinos with food assistance. The donation should provide 1.4 million meals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221"><a href="#cite_note-221">[217]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/IKEA" title="IKEA">IKEA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Walmart" title="Walmart">Walmart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Samsung" title="Samsung">Samsung</a>, and <a href="/wiki/HSBC" title="HSBC">HSBC</a> are among those taking advantage of the event to donate to those in need.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222"><a href="#cite_note-222">[218]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223"><a href="#cite_note-223">[219]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Northwestern_Mutual" title="Northwestern Mutual">Northwestern Mutual</a> announced they will donate $100,000 to the <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">American Red Cross</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-prnewswire_224-0"><a href="#cite_note-prnewswire-224">[220]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/The_Coca-Cola_Company" title="The Coca-Cola Company">The Coca-Cola Company</a> says they have donated $2.5 million of their advertising budget to the relief efforts as of November 25.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-huffpostnov35_225-0"><a href="#cite_note-huffpostnov35-225">[221]</a></sup> By mid-December <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> donated $1 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-226"><a href="#cite_note-226">[222]</a></sup> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/DHL" title="DHL">DHL</a> deployed its Asia Pacific Disaster Response Team to the disaster areas to provide on-the-ground logistics support to assist with the relief effort in the aftermath of the devastating Typhoon Haiyan. Three rotating teams made up of volunteer employees from the Asia Pacific region were based at the Mactan Cebu Airport on Cebu island, providing support and assistance to the country's most affected areas west of Leyte Island, including Guiuan, Roxas, and Tacloban city.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-227"><a href="#cite_note-227">[223]</a></sup> Many smaller initiatives were founded as well - e.g. to prepare by donating to children a typhoon-ready backpack as floating device.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228"><a href="#cite_note-228">[224]</a></sup></p>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1365" data-file-width="2048" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/220px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/330px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg/440px-US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:US_marines_Typhoon_Haiyan_relief.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Marines" title="U.S. Marines">U.S. Marines</a> assisting in the Philippine disaster relief.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>Sixteen-time <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NBA" title="NBA">NBA</a> Champions <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Lakers" title="Los Angeles Lakers">Los Angeles Lakers</a> donated $150,000 <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229"><a href="#cite_note-229">[225]</a></sup> to the <a href="/wiki/Philippine_Red_Cross" title="Philippine Red Cross">Philippine Red Cross</a> to aid the typhoon affected victims. During their home game against the <a href="/wiki/Memphis_Grizzlies" title="Memphis Grizzlies">Memphis Grizzlies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kobe_Bryant" title="Kobe Bryant">Kobe Bryant</a> handed the check to the Junior <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NBA" title="NBA">NBA</a> players representing the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. His teammate, <a href="/wiki/Pau_Gasol" title="Pau Gasol">Pau Gasol</a>, pledged to donate $1,000 per point to UNICEF<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230"><a href="#cite_note-230">[226]</a></sup> with the directive to help victims of Super Typhoon Haiyan in the country as well. He scored 24 points in a won game against the <a href="/wiki/Golden_State_Warriors" title="Golden State Warriors">Golden State Warriors</a>. <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Baseball" title="Major League Baseball">Major League Baseball</a> donated $200,000 to <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> and the American Red Cross, with <a href="/wiki/Commissioner_of_Baseball" title="Commissioner of Baseball">Commissioner</a> <a href="/wiki/Bud_Selig" title="Bud Selig">Bud Selig</a> encouraging fans to donate to the organizations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mlb_231-0"><a href="#cite_note-mlb-231">[227]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> delivered portable toilets and hygiene supplies to the region and also appealed for $34 million to help the four million children affected.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-232"><a href="#cite_note-232">[228]</a></sup> The American Red Cross announced that they collected $11 million in donations for the Philippines Relief Fund.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233"><a href="#cite_note-233">[229]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Mercy_Corps" title="Mercy Corps">Mercy Corps</a> dispatched a "emergency response" team to help with humanitarian efforts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-theoregonian_234-0"><a href="#cite_note-theoregonian-234">[230]</a></sup> MAP International launched medical relief efforts providing over $10 million in medicines and supplies to the Philippines.</p>
<p>Among the NGO responses, among the most comprehensive disaster response came from the Taiwan-based <cite class="citation web"><a class="external text" href="http://www.tzuchi.org.ph/newsite/" rel="nofollow">"Buddhist Tzu Chi Foundation"</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATyphoon+Haiyan&amp;rft.btitle=Buddhist+Tzu+Chi+Foundation&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.tzuchi.org.ph%2Fnewsite%2F&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook"><span style="display:none;"> </span></span>, which organized a large-scale cash-for-work program in Tacloban from Nov 20 to Dec 8 with up to 31,000 participants per day, totaling nearly 300,000 day shifts. This operation not only helped clean out the thousands of tons of debris covering the city, but also kick-started the local economy. Tzu Chi also contributed emergency cash aid of 8000, 12000 or 15000 pesos depending on family size for over 60,000 families in the affected areas of Tacloban, Ormoc, Palo, Tanauan and Tunga, and has been providing free clinics, hot meals, and temporary class rooms for over 15 schools in the area. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doctors_Without_Borders" title="Doctors Without Borders">Doctors Without Borders</a> is sending 200 tons of aid.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-world-asia-24901993_214-1"><a href="#cite_note-world-asia-24901993-214">[210]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-news24_235-0"><a href="#cite_note-news24-235">[231]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/International_Society_for_Krishna_Consciousness" title="International Society for Krishna Consciousness">International Society for Krishna Consciousness</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Food_For_Life_Global" title="Food For Life Global">Food For Life Global</a>, the world's largest vegan food relief organisation, raised money and provided vegan meals in the Philippines to Typhoon Haiyan survivors.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-236"><a href="#cite_note-236">[232]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-237"><a href="#cite_note-237">[233]</a></sup> Other NGOs run by faith-based organisations that raised money and/or aided in the disaster relief efforts of Typhoon Haiyan included <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Relief_Services" title="Catholic Relief Services">Catholic Relief Services</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-0"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> Catholic Medical Mission Board (CMMB),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-1"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Adventist_Development_and_Relief_Agency" title="Adventist Development and Relief Agency">Adventist Development and Relief Agency</a> (ADRA),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-2"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> LDS Philanthropies,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-239"><a href="#cite_note-239">[235]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/American_Jewish_Joint_Distribution_Committee" title="American Jewish Joint Distribution Committee">American Jewish Joint Distribution Committee</a> (AJJDC),<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-3"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Samaritan%27s_Purse" title="Samaritan's Purse">Samaritan's Purse</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-4"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Salvation_Army" title="Salvation Army">Salvation Army</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-5"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Christian_Children%27s_Fund_of_Canada" title="Christian Children's Fund of Canada">Christian Children's Fund of Canada</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-6"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/MAP_International" title="MAP International">MAP International</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Vision" title="World Vision">World Vision</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNNHaiyan_238-7"><a href="#cite_note-CNNHaiyan-238">[234]</a></sup></p>
<p>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iglesia_Ni_Cristo" title="Iglesia Ni Cristo">Iglesia Ni Cristo</a> (INC), the largest indigenous Christian church based in the Philippines held series of massive relief distributions and medical and dental missions to affected population of the storm to different parts of <a href="/wiki/Visayas" title="Visayas">Visayas</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240"><a href="#cite_note-240">[236]</a></sup> The humanitarian mission was done under the <a class="external text" href="http://www.kabayankokapatidko.org/" rel="nofollow">"Lingap sa Mamamayan" (Aid for Humanity)</a> project in cooperation with the Felix Y. Manalo (FYM) Foundation Inc., the INC’s charitable arm.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-241"><a href="#cite_note-241">[237]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242"><a href="#cite_note-242">[238]</a></sup> The church conducted the largest walk for a cause in the world (<a href="/wiki/Walkathon" title="Walkathon">walkathon</a>) on February 15, 2014, dubbed as 'Iglesia Ni Cristo World Wide Walk for Those Affected by Typhoon Yolanda/Haiyan'.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-243"><a href="#cite_note-243">[239]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-244"><a href="#cite_note-244">[240]</a></sup> The walk for a cause raised millions of money to help the victims of the super typhoon for the construction of their houses and shelters. The aim of the activity is to make the world understand that Haiyan survivors are still in dare need of help and financial assistance. Indeed, the worldwide walk caught the attention of the world when it breaks two <a href="/wiki/Guinness" title="Guinness">Guinness</a> world records as the largest charity walk in a single venue (<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Manila,_Philippines" title="Manila, Philippines">Manila, Philippines</a>) with 175,000 participants, and largest charity walk in 24 hours for multiple venues (from <a href="/wiki/Christchurch" title="Christchurch">Christchurch</a>, New Zealand to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hawaii,_USA" title="Hawaii, USA">Hawaii, USA</a>) in 13 time zones, 54 countries, 24 hours with 519, 521 participants.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-245"><a href="#cite_note-245">[241]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-246"><a href="#cite_note-246">[242]</a></sup></p>
<p>Celebrities such as <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham" title="David Beckham">David</a> and <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Beckham</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-247"><a href="#cite_note-247">[243]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Colbert" title="Stephen Colbert">Stephen Colbert</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-248"><a href="#cite_note-248">[244]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Kim_Kardashian" title="Kim Kardashian">Kim Kardashian</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-249"><a href="#cite_note-249">[245]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/David_Guetta" title="David Guetta">David Guetta</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-250"><a href="#cite_note-250">[246]</a></sup> and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_X_Factor_(TV_series)" title="The X Factor (TV series)">The X Factor</a></i> contributed to the fundraising.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-251"><a href="#cite_note-251">[247]</a></sup> On November 26, <a href="/wiki/ITunes" title="ITunes">iTunes</a> released a <a href="/wiki/Compilation_album" title="Compilation album">compilation album</a> entitled <i>Songs for the Philippines</i> featuring different artists, including <a href="/wiki/Katy_Perry" title="Katy Perry">Katy Perry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Madonna_(entertainer)" title="Madonna (entertainer)">Madonna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bob_Dylan" title="Bob Dylan">Bob Dylan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/The_Beatles" title="The Beatles">The Beatles</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usatodaynov25_252-0"><a href="#cite_note-usatodaynov25-252">[248]</a></sup> All proceeds will go to the <a href="/wiki/Philippine_Red_Cross" title="Philippine Red Cross">Philippine Red Cross</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usatodaynov25_252-1"><a href="#cite_note-usatodaynov25-252">[248]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/OneRepublic" title="OneRepublic">OneRepublic</a> donated $100,000 on November 30, 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-253"><a href="#cite_note-253">[249]</a></sup> Other celebrities that offered their support included <a href="/wiki/Linkin_Park" title="Linkin Park">Linkin Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/The_Offspring" title="The Offspring">The Offspring</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-254"><a href="#cite_note-254">[250]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Keys" title="Alicia Keys">Alicia Keys</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-255"><a href="#cite_note-255">[251]</a></sup> and Justin Bieber.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-256"><a href="#cite_note-256">[252]</a></sup></p>
<p>On the day of his death, actor <a href="/wiki/Paul_Walker" title="Paul Walker">Paul Walker</a> attended a charity event for his organization, Reach Out Worldwide, for the victims of the typhoon that was held right before his accident.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CNN1_257-0"><a href="#cite_note-CNN1-257">[253]</a></sup></p>
<p>On March 11, 2014, a benefit concert called <a class="external text" href="http://www.pinoyrelief.com/pinoyconcert" rel="nofollow">The Pinoy Relief Benefit Concert</a> was held at <a href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden" title="Madison Square Garden">Madison Square Garden</a> in New York, City. <a href="/wiki/Jennifer_Hudson" title="Jennifer Hudson">Jennifer Hudson</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pentatonix" title="Pentatonix">Pentatonix</a>, <a href="/wiki/A_Great_Big_World" title="A Great Big World">A Great Big World</a>, <a href="/wiki/Plain_White_T%27s" title="Plain White T's">Plain White T's</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jessica_Sanchez" title="Jessica Sanchez">Jessica Sanchez</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charice" title="Charice">Charice</a> and REO Brothers performed. Special guests also included <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dr._Oz" title="Dr. Oz">Dr. Oz</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dante_Basco" title="Dante Basco">Dante Basco</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bobby_Lopez" title="Bobby Lopez">Bobby Lopez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kristen_Anderson-Lopez" title="Kristen Anderson-Lopez">Kristen Anderson-Lopez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Apl.de.ap" title="Apl.de.ap">Apl.de.ap</a>. 100% of proceeds raised directly went to the Typhoon Haiyan survivors.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-258"><a href="#cite_note-258">[254]</a></sup> <a class="external text" href="http://www.pinoyrelief.com" rel="nofollow">Pinoy Relief</a> was created to help survivors and focus on three specific areas: restoring livelihoods, building classrooms and providing shelter in partnership with local NGOs, <a href="/wiki/Habitat_for_Humanity" title="Habitat for Humanity">Habitat for Humanity</a> Philippines and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Operation_Blessing" title="Operation Blessing">Operation Blessing</a> Philippines.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-259"><a href="#cite_note-259">[255]</a></sup></p>
<p>On March 13, 2016, former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_of_America" title="United States of America">United States of America</a> vice president <a href="/wiki/Al_Gore" title="Al Gore">Al Gore</a>, visited Tacloban and delivered his speech in front of the survivors of Haiyan. He also dropped by at the MV Eva Jocelyn, a cargo ship that washed out inland during the typhoon and now converted into a memorial park.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-260"><a href="#cite_note-260">[256]</a></sup></p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Politics_involving_aid_relief">Politics involving aid relief</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Politics involving aid relief">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu,_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3744" data-file-width="5616" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/220px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/330px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/97/First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg/440px-First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu%2C_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:First_UK-funded_humanitarian_flight_arrives_in_Cebu,_Philippines_-_10826427444.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
First UK-funded humanitarian flight arrives at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mactan-Cebu_International_Airport" title="Mactan-Cebu International Airport">Mactan-Cebu International Airport</a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2400" data-file-width="3600" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/220px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/330px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/10/Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg/440px-Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Philippine_island_of_Binuluanguan_Following_Typhoon_Haiyan_MOD_45156472.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The island of Binuluanguan overflown by a helicopter from HMS <i>Daring</i>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The aid contributions of China and the United States were given focus with regards to their involvement in the politics of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-261"><a href="#cite_note-261">[257]</a></sup> Apart from having the two largest economies in the world, both countries are involved in a complex relationship with the island country. China is currently <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spratly_islands_dispute" title="Spratly islands dispute">disputing</a> the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> in the <a href="/wiki/South_China_Sea" title="South China Sea">South China Sea</a> with the Philippines while the United States used to be an occupying power and currently has a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mutual_Defense_Treaty_(U.S.%E2%80%93Philippines)" title="Mutual Defense Treaty (U.S.–Philippines)">mutual defense treaty with the islands</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-262"><a href="#cite_note-262">[258]</a></sup></p>
<p>China was initially criticized for its meager contribution of US $100,000 cash each from the government and the Chinese Red Cross to the typhoon victims, which led to commentary about its disputes with the Philippines.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-263"><a href="#cite_note-263">[259]</a></sup> Earlier in 2013, <a href="/wiki/Philippines_v._China" title="Philippines v. China">the Philippines sued China</a> over the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nine-dotted_line" title="Nine-dotted line">nine-dotted line</a>. Commentators attribute this low amount to China's intentions to isolate the Philippines while strengthening its ties with the rest of Southeast Asia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-264"><a href="#cite_note-264">[260]</a></sup> The move had mixed reactions from the public of China with some commending its decision while others, such as <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Global_Times" title="The Global Times">The Global Times</a></i>, insisted that China should be a responsible power. China later increased its contributions by US$1.64 million in supplies <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-China_Increases_Aid_to_Philippines_140-1"><a href="#cite_note-China_Increases_Aid_to_Philippines-140">[136]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-265"><a href="#cite_note-265">[261]</a></sup> and sent its naval hospital ship <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Peace_Ark" title="Peace Ark">Peace Ark</a></i> for disaster relief."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-peace-ark_141-1"><a href="#cite_note-peace-ark-141">[137]</a></sup></p>
<p>The contributions of the United States was in contrast to that of China. It gave the Philippines an amount of US$51.9 million worth of aid apart and deployed the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Marines" title="United States Marines">United States Marines</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> in order to assist with the humanitarian operations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-266"><a href="#cite_note-266">[262]</a></sup> This was seen by observers as part of the Asia pivot that the United States government had previously announced.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-267"><a href="#cite_note-267">[263]</a></sup> The Philippine government had been discussing with the U.S. plans regarding the deployment of U.S. military troops within the country. Aid contributions of the U.S. was seen as a sign of goodwill in order to further strengthen relations.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-268"><a href="#cite_note-268">[264]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Vietnam_3">Vietnam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Vietnam">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Following Typhoon Haiyan's landfall in Vietnam, widespread search and rescue missions took place in the affected provinces. Damage assessments were also conducted in 13 provinces to determine what aid was needed. The IFRC began distribution of relief supplies and assisted residents in returning home by November 12. Operations regarding the aftermath of Typhoon Wutip were temporarily suspended due to Haiyan.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-VietnamRW2_51-3"><a href="#cite_note-VietnamRW2-51">[48]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Climate_change">Climate change</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Climate change">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Political leaders and climate scientists <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_global_warming" title="Effects of global warming">connected</a> the typhoon to <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">climate change</a>, both at the time and subsequently<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-269"><a href="#cite_note-269">[265]</a></sup> and led to calls for climate justice.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-270"><a href="#cite_note-270">[266]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/2013_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference">2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference</a> was coincidentally in progress when the typhoon struck and Yeb Saño, the lead negotiator of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> delegation, received a standing ovation at the conference when he declared a hunger strike.</p>
<blockquote class="templatequote">
<p>In solidarity with my countrymen who are struggling to find food back home, I will now commence a voluntary fasting for the climate; this means I will voluntarily refrain from eating food during this <a href="/wiki/2013_United_Nations_Climate_Change_Conference" title="2013 United Nations Climate Change Conference">COP</a>, until a meaningful outcome is in sight.</p>
<div class="templatequotecite">— <cite>Yeb Saño<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-271"><a href="#cite_note-271">[267]</a></sup></cite></div>
</blockquote>
<p>Several delegates, including American delegate Collin Reese, joined him in fasting. Sixty people from <a href="/wiki/Climate_Action_Network" title="Climate Action Network">Climate Action Network</a>, an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Umbrella_group" title="Umbrella group">umbrella group</a> of environmental non-governmental organisations, also joined the hunger strike.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-272"><a href="#cite_note-272">[268]</a></sup></p>
<p>The correlation between the increasing intensity of storms and the progression of climate change was discussed by climate scientists. "Typhoons, hurricanes and all tropical storms draw their vast energy from the warmth of the sea. We know sea-surface temperatures are warming pretty much around the planet, so that's a pretty direct influence of climate change on the nature of the storm," said <a href="/wiki/Will_Steffen" title="Will Steffen">Will Steffen</a>, director of the <a href="/wiki/Australian_National_University" title="Australian National University">Australian National University</a> climate change institute.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-0"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Myles_Allen" title="Myles Allen">Myles Allen</a>, head of the climate dynamics group at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Oxford" title="University of Oxford">University of Oxford</a>, said that "The current consensus is that climate change is not making the risk of hurricanes any greater, but there are physical arguments and evidence that there is a risk of more intense hurricanes."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-1"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup> <i>The Huffington Post</i> made the point that the 70% <a href="/wiki/Deforestation_in_the_Philippines" title="Deforestation in the Philippines">deforestation of the Philippines</a> since 1900, as reported by the national <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Environment_and_Natural_Resources_(Philippines)" title="Department of Environment and Natural Resources (Philippines)">Forest Management Bureau</a>, made far more lethal flooding from cyclones like Haiyan more likely.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-274"><a href="#cite_note-274">[270]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/IPCC_Fifth_Assessment_Report" title="IPCC Fifth Assessment Report">IPCC Fifth Assessment Report</a> had stated in September of the same year that "Time series of cyclone indices such as power dissipation, an aggregate compound of tropical cyclone frequency, duration, and intensity that measures total wind energy by tropical cyclones, show upward trends in the North Atlantic and weaker upward trends in the western North Pacific since the late 1970s."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian-13-11-12_273-2"><a href="#cite_note-Guardian-13-11-12-273">[269]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_media">In popular media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: In popular media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A detailed analysis of Typhoon Haiyan and its destruction in the Philippines was featured in a documentary called <i>Megastorm: World's Biggest Typhoon</i>. It aired on December 30, 2013 on <a href="/wiki/Discovery_Channel" title="Discovery Channel">Discovery Channel</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-275"><a href="#cite_note-275">[271]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Typhoon_Haiyan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: See also">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li id="cite_note-9"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-9">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/Joint_Typhoon_Warning_Center" title="Joint Typhoon Warning Center">Joint Typhoon Warning Center</a> is a joint <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">United States Navy</a> – <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">United States Air Force</a> task force that issues tropical cyclone warnings for the western Pacific Ocean and other regions.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></span></li>
<li id="cite_note-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-13">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/Japan_Meteorological_Agency" title="Japan Meteorological Agency">Japan Meteorological Agency</a> (JMA) is the official <a href="/wiki/Regional_Specialized_Meteorological_Center" title="Regional Specialized Meteorological Center">Regional Specialized Meteorological Center</a> for the western Pacific Ocean.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup></span></li>

<li id="cite_note-damage-55"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-damage_55-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><b>Total damages</b> figure includes agriculture, infrastructure, casualties, etc. damages.</span></li>
